		focus = POR_strengthening_regime_pvde

			x = -39
			y = 0
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = POR_revolt_against_salazar_regime
			}
		}
		offset = {
			x = -15
			y = 0
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = POR_formation_of_popular_front
			}
		}
		offset = {
			x = -5
			y = 0
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = POR_restoration_of_monarchy
					has_completed_focus = POR_victory_of_portuguese_communist_party

						has_completed_focus = POR_maintain_neutrality_in_spanish_war
						has_completed_focus = POR_formation_of_popular_front
					}
				}
			}
		}
		offset = {
			x = -39
			y = 0
			trigger = {

			}
		}

							target = PREV
							type = annex_everything
							expire = 0
						}
						hidden_effect = {
							add_ai_strategy = {
								type = antagonize
								id = PREV
								value = 200
							}
							add_ai_strategy = {
								type = declare_war
								id = PREV
								value = 100
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { global.spain_cores = THIS }
						owner = {
							NOT = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					owner = {
						ROOT = {
							create_wargoal = {
								target = PREV

								expire = 0
							}

					add_core_of = PREV
				}
				every_state = {

					}
					remove_core_of = PREV
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { global.spain_cores = THIS }
						NOT = { is_controlled_by = PREV }
						is_claimed_by = PREV

					}

							building = dockyard

						type = dockyard		
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_core_of = ROOT
						free_building_slots = {
							building = dockyard
							size > 1
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
